  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_7be21ddf-c313-4efa-9a4c-44fd99d652e7'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13460432-anovelqueen?shelf=insta-love">insta-love</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3574458021" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer447121259910776992">***4 STARS***<br/><br/>What a great continuation of Logan &Emily’s love story.<br/><br/>Emily sacrificed herself and her freedom in order to help her newfound family. It is a sacrifice she is willing to make because of the outcome but it is difficult for her to endure. Emily has to fight the world her father puts before her...a life that she wishes to put behind her. Emily has dyslexia and her father feels like she is stupid and can only be a rich man’s wife but Emily loves her music and she loves Logan even more. </span>
  <span id="freeText447121259910776992" style="display:none">***4 STARS***<br /><br />What a great continuation of Logan &amp;Emily’s love story.<br /><br />Emily sacrificed herself and her freedom in order to help her newfound family. It is a sacrifice she is willing to make because of the outcome but it is difficult for her to endure. Emily has to fight the world her father puts before her...a life that she wishes to put behind her. Emily has dyslexia and her father feels like she is stupid and can only be a rich man’s wife but Emily loves her music and she loves Logan even more. They have been separated for three months and Logan has returned to college. <br /><br />I was more vested in this story as many of the pieces fell into place. Logan and Emily continue to have to overcome obstacles particularly from her world in order to prove to others that they love one another. It is a lovely story and really builds up anticipation for the other Reed Brothers in finding their HEA. I am in it for the long haul...gotta finish the series! </span>
  <a data-text-id="447121259910776992" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/680888689" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/680888689?book_show_action=true">Jul 29, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer680888689" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16962059312968953599"><b>4 I heart Logan stars!</b><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/dbeabbe5-3a65-4cfc-872b-dcc2abdd9c79_zpsaadbf9e1.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431082i/864794.jpg' alt=' photo dbeabbe5-3a65-4cfc-872b-dcc2abdd9c79_zpsaadbf9e1.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><i>Smart, Sexy, and Secretive</i> leaves off three months after Emily left NY in TTT. It’s been three months since she has seen or spoken too Logan. But now she is back in NYC for good. No one could keep her away from him. <br/><b>
  <blockquote>New York is where my heart is. It’s where Logan is.</blockquote>
</b><br/>Logan has been waiting for the day that Emily comes back to him. He appreciates all she’s done, the sacrifices she made for him and his family, but he misses her like crazy. Once he gets her back, he’s n</span>
  <span id="freeText16962059312968953599" style="display:none"><b>4 I heart Logan stars!</b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/dbeabbe5-3a65-4cfc-872b-dcc2abdd9c79_zpsaadbf9e1.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431082i/864794.jpg" alt=" photo dbeabbe5-3a65-4cfc-872b-dcc2abdd9c79_zpsaadbf9e1.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>Smart, Sexy, and Secretive</i> leaves off three months after Emily left NY in TTT. It’s been three months since she has seen or spoken too Logan. But now she is back in NYC for good. No one could keep her away from him. <br><b>
  <blockquote>New York is where my heart is. It’s where Logan is.</blockquote>
</b><br>Logan has been waiting for the day that Emily comes back to him. He appreciates all she’s done, the sacrifices she made for him and his family, but he misses her like crazy. Once he gets her back, he’s never letting her go. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/d507a2a2-8380-45a2-b4a4-d7e34d130653_zps915c2623.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431082i/864795.jpg" alt=" photo d507a2a2-8380-45a2-b4a4-d7e34d130653_zps915c2623.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Logan and Emily are a sensational couple. I adore them together. Their relationship has obstacles, and not just the hearing impairment/dyslexia. Emily’s father and ex-boyfriend are both big issues. Emily’s father thinks he knows what is best for Emily, and he wants her no where near someone like Logan. He ex is just a giant douchebag. Thankfully, Emily’s mom is able to smooth things over a few times. <br><br>I also just loved that Emily learned more sign language. She wanted to be able to communicate better with Logan. The elevator scene with the nurse was pretty funny. And did I mention that I LOVE LOGAN?!?! Because I do! <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/812a5a35-1ab4-4c3d-8111-22939caffb1e_zpsc6693dde.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431082i/864796.jpg" alt=" photo 812a5a35-1ab4-4c3d-8111-22939caffb1e_zpsc6693dde.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Emily and Logan truly love each other. They are one anothers forever. Thankfully, with all the outside drama going on (and there was a TON of drama) there wasn’t any Logan/Emily drama. They were just focused on dealing with everything- together. I was happy with the closure Emily got with her father and the music. It was good to see. I liked the ending, but it felt a little rushed. I wish we would have gotten more of an epilogue.<br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/ff56c5ce-4766-45ff-a676-7740eda3e9fc_zpsba6365bf.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431082i/864797.jpg" alt=" photo ff56c5ce-4766-45ff-a676-7740eda3e9fc_zpsba6365bf.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>My biggest complaint about this story is that it took me less than two hours to read it. I WANTED MORE!!!! It’s such a great NA read. Logan is an amazing guy, and I love Emily too. <br><br>Engaging, comical, sweet, sexy, endearing and just an overall great read! Looking forward to the next installment of this series (One of Logan’s brothers). Hopefully we see more of Emily and Logan! A short, steamy and enjoyable series I would recommend!!! </span>
  <a data-text-id="16962059312968953599" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2918130012?book_show_action=true">Aug 19, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ꮗ€♫◗☿ ❤️ ilikebooksbest.com ❤️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ꮗ€♫◗☿ ❤️ ilikebooksbest.com ❤️" href="/user/show/70316517-ilikebooksbest-com">Ꮗ€♫◗☿ ❤️ ilikebooksbest.com ❤️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/70316517-ilikebooksbest-com?shelf=erotic-romance">erotic-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/70316517-ilikebooksbest-com?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2918130012" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9440391407477385214"><strong>I am loving these guys and this series!</strong><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1566275446ra/28019269.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I know right now I will have to end up reading many more of these books. The way the supporting characters are written, you just end up loving them all as much as the two main characters you are reading about. So I want to know how each of the Reed Brothers finds their one true love. Since there are more books than there are brothers, I expect these will go further into friends, cousins and the like. I probably will want to read the entire series if they ar</span>
  <span id="freeText9440391407477385214" style="display:none"><strong>I am loving these guys and this series!</strong><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1566275446ra/28019269.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I know right now I will have to end up reading many more of these books. The way the supporting characters are written, you just end up loving them all as much as the two main characters you are reading about. So I want to know how each of the Reed Brothers finds their one true love. Since there are more books than there are brothers, I expect these will go further into friends, cousins and the like. I probably will want to read the entire series if they are as good as these first two books.<br><br>This book was every bit as good as book #1. It was a continuation of the story of Logan Reed and his girl Emily. Though at the end of book 1, Emily had gone home to her father in return for her father agreeing to get Logan’s brother Matt a special cancer treatment that was extremely costly. The boys couldn’t afford the treatment and Matt’s life expectancy without it was not good.<br><br>This book has her returning to New York to attend Juilliard while Logan attends NYU for Art and Advertising. Though as far as her fathers concerned, Logan is poor and not good enough for her and Juilliard is just a waste of time, since studying music has nothing to do with the real world. <br><br>Her father wants her to marry her ex fiancé Trip. They both think she is stupid due to her dyslexia and is unable to learn because she can’t read. Her father thinks the best she can attain is to marry well and Logan doesn’t fit the bill. So though he allows her to move to New York and sets her up in a nice apartment, he has some surprises in store to keep her and Logan apart.<br><br>The story is great, the twists and turns are perfect. Some are predictable, but with non-predictable outcomes. Some are completely out of left field and those are the best and sometimes worst kind. But you gotta love them either way. Tammy Falkner is good at giving exactly what I want but enough surprises so that it isn’t the same as other things I have read.<br><br>Emily and Logan have true love for each other and stick together which is nice to see. I like the, as a couple and hw they each make their disabilities a non issue. I can’t wait to dive into more of this series.<br> <br><a href="https://www.ilikebooksbest.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a>|<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/wennel" rel="nofollow noopener">Goodreads</a>|<a href="https://www.facebook.com/ilikebooksbest" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a>|<a href="https://smile.amazon.com/gp/profile/amzn1.account.AFFE5A2BGXJQTQMCYHFC4YHV6KFQ?preview=true" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon</a>|<a href="https://www.twitter.com/wendysu020202" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a>|<a href="https://www.bookbub.com/profile/1895823057" rel="nofollow noopener">BookBub</a></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer683102419" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17591121201601506631">4.5--<b>I Want My Own Logan</b>--Stars!!!!<br/><br/>Logan, Logan, Logan.....<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380431394ra/865677.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>SSaS picks up three months after TTaT when Emily returned home to her father in exchange for Matt's cancer treatment. Emily has returned to NY and is committed to getting Logan back. <br/><br/>I loved that it didn't take forever for Logan and Emily to get back together. That they were both faithful to each other while they were apart. When they final reunited it was like they were never apart. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380431394ra/865678.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Emily's parents are in town....her dad is TROUBLE! I d</span>
  <span id="freeText17591121201601506631" style="display:none">4.5--<b>I Want My Own Logan</b>--Stars!!!!<br><br>Logan, Logan, Logan.....<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380431394ra/865677.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>SSaS picks up three months after TTaT when Emily returned home to her father in exchange for Matt's cancer treatment. Emily has returned to NY and is committed to getting Logan back. <br><br>I loved that it didn't take forever for Logan and Emily to get back together. That they were both faithful to each other while they were apart. When they final reunited it was like they were never apart. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380431394ra/865678.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Emily's parents are in town....her dad is TROUBLE! I did not like him at all. Emily also has an unexpected visitor trying to come between her and Logan. I also really liked how the author didn't create drama between Logan and Emily but rather had them deal with her dad and the unexpected visitor. <br><br>Logan is now taking classes at NYU and Emily is going to Julliard. Logan and Emily are trying to win her dad over. For Logan, he wants him to see how much he loves Emily and how perfect she is for him. For Emily, she just wants him to see her as someone smart and worthy. Not just arm candy for some jerk. <br><br>Her first school performance changes everything for Emily. She's able to share her love of music with both her dad and Logan. It was really a beautiful moment. Only to be followed up with....<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380431394ra/865679.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>A big WTF just happened??? <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380425101ra/847988.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Listen Tammy....that was a real shitty thing to do. LOL!<br><br>Bottomline, this was a great follow-up to Logan and Emily's story. I would say it had more of a HFN ending versus a HEA. I am hoping there are more books in the series--possibly about the other Reed brothers. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I need to know what happens to Pete!! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> And obvs I hope we get more of Logan and Emily. <br><br>My only complaint would be that I wish these books were longer!! </["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer684456722" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16753014341559666300"><a href='http://s725.photobucket.com/user/Kristin90183/media/GR%20Stuff/doitagain.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/623704.gif' alt=' photo doitagain.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/>Another wonderful experience with Emily & Logan and the Reed clan, was had by all!!! I give this one 4.5 stars. Mainly because it was a little short in my opinion, there was some predictability to some of the elements, some repetitiveness, and some things seemed to happen a little to abruptly. But I much rather a story I am loving be too short a little predictable and quick rather than the opposite, hence only the .5 deduction. <br/><br/><br/><a href='http://s725.photobucket.com/user/Kristin90183/media/GR%20Stuff/love.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431585i/866133.jpg' alt=' photo love.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>We pick up three months later and it doesn't take forever an</span>
  <span id="freeText16753014341559666300" style="display:none"><a href="http://s725.photobucket.com/user/Kristin90183/media/GR%20Stuff/doitagain.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/623704.gif" alt=" photo doitagain.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Another wonderful experience with Emily &amp; Logan and the Reed clan, was had by all!!! I give this one 4.5 stars. Mainly because it was a little short in my opinion, there was some predictability to some of the elements, some repetitiveness, and some things seemed to happen a little to abruptly. But I much rather a story I am loving be too short a little predictable and quick rather than the opposite, hence only the .5 deduction. <br><br><br><a href="http://s725.photobucket.com/user/Kristin90183/media/GR%20Stuff/love.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431585i/866133.jpg" alt=" photo love.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>We pick up three months later and it doesn't take forever and a day for Emily and Logan to find their way back to each other. (I loved that too!) We had plenty of time to focus on their relationship. They work really well together in difficult situations and I really enjoyed how they stuck together when times got tough. The issues that caused anxiety were dealt with somewhat quickly and did not drag out leaving you pulling your hair out. I think it was just the right balance of drama and angst. I am so very excited to read more about the Reed brothers in the future and hope to get some glimpses into how Emily and Logan are doing later on. This book left me with lots of warm and fuzzy feelings and I suggest this series for anyone who wants a great dynamic story that will make you tear up and get angry but in the end walk away with a smile on your face.<br><br><a href="http://s725.photobucket.com/user/Kristin90183/media/GR%20Stuff/youandme.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431585i/866135._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo LOGANANDEMILY.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s725.photobucket.com/user/Kristin90183/media/GR%20Stuff/truelove.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431020i/864659.jpg" alt=" photo truelove.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<div id="review_719657650" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/719657650" />
    <a title="Karla" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3024056-karla"><img alt="Karla" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1324910771p2/3024056.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/719657650?book_show_action=true">Sep 14, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Karla" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Karla" href="/user/show/3024056-karla">Karla</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=family-drama">family-drama</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=emotional">emotional</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=wonderful-secondary-characters">wonderful-secondary-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=2-points-of-view">2-points-of-view</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=terrific-dialogue">terrific-dialogue</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=bevy-of-scrumptious-brothers">bevy-of-scrumptious-brothers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=determined-heroine">determined-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=character-we-love-from-the-past">character-we-love-from-the-past</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=continuing-story">continuing-story</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer719657650" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8955377123850771263"><br/><b> 4 Strong Stars! I'm very happy with the direction this book took.</b><br/><br/>Could this have all been wrapped up in one book? Yes, I believe so, but it also could have gone very bad, and yet it didn't. I'm not a fan of author's dragging couple drama from one book to the next, but that was not the case here. There was drama, don't get me wrong and some of it a little over the top, but as far as Logan and Emily were concerned...they were <b>solid</b>, no back and forth, they find common ground and stand together as</span>
  <span id="freeText8955377123850771263" style="display:none"><br /><b> 4 Strong Stars! I'm very happy with the direction this book took.</b><br /><br />Could this have all been wrapped up in one book? Yes, I believe so, but it also could have gone very bad, and yet it didn't. I'm not a fan of author's dragging couple drama from one book to the next, but that was not the case here. There was drama, don't get me wrong and some of it a little over the top, but as far as Logan and Emily were concerned...they were <b>solid</b>, no back and forth, they find common ground and stand together as one, and I loved that!! <br /><br />I adore Logan and Emily, and even though they are dealing with their own struggles as a couple, they are perfect for each other. The love is strong, very strong between these two, and you feel it every time they are together. The involvement of both of their families added some additional layers to the story, although I could have done with out one or two scenes involving Emily's family...her father in particular. He's unbelievably ridiculous and one disastrous scene at the end might have gone a little too far for my taste. Then again, I was flipping pages like a mad woman, so maybe I liked the drama. I admit it, I was sucked in. Funny how that happens. <br /><br />To the author's credit, she is actually giving you two books in one. Each book in the series has a sexy-lite version, with suggestive, not descriptive sex, or you can read full out steam! So, the reader gets to choose. The author did this for her son, who was not comfortable reading the steamier version, but wanted to read his mother's books. She passed it on to us...we get to choose. So, even though initially I felt that books 1 and 2 could have been released as one book, there is a method to Tammy Falkner's madness. She didn't make us wait forever for book 2, which I appreciated, and you get your money's worth, whether or not she offered up both versions. I hope she continues to do this with the other books as the series moves forward. <br /><br />I'm hooked on this series and most especially the Reed brothers. You can see the writing on the wall for some of the characters, but one thing is for sure, it's proving to be an addictive series that doesn't just focus on one couple, this is about family!</span>
  <a data-text-id="8955377123850771263" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1215897378" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1215897378" />
    <a title="Brenna" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12928663-brenna"><img alt="Brenna" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1580475762p2/12928663.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1215897378?book_show_action=true">Mar 01, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Brenna" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Brenna" href="/user/show/12928663-brenna">Brenna</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12928663-brenna?shelf=romantic">romantic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12928663-brenna?shelf=audible">audible</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12928663-brenna?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12928663-brenna?shelf=drove-me-crazy">drove-me-crazy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1215897378" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3569273932458486722"><i>Smart, Sexy, and Secretive</i> is the continuation of Logan and Emily’s story. Following on from Emily going back to California, Logan is left in New York wondering if/when Emily is coming back. Thankfully things move very quickly and soon they are back together, with very minimal drama involved in the reunion, which I was very happy about. It’s clear that they are still very much in love and want nothing more than to be together. <br/><i>
  <blockquote> “Loved you then. Love you now.” </blockquote>
</i><br/>Unfortunately, Emily’s father do</span>
  <span id="freeText3569273932458486722" style="display:none"><i>Smart, Sexy, and Secretive</i> is the continuation of Logan and Emily’s story. Following on from Emily going back to California, Logan is left in New York wondering if/when Emily is coming back. Thankfully things move very quickly and soon they are back together, with very minimal drama involved in the reunion, which I was very happy about. It’s clear that they are still very much in love and want nothing more than to be together. <br /><i>
  <blockquote> “Loved you then. Love you now.” </blockquote>
</i><br />Unfortunately, Emily’s father doesn’t approve of Logan at all. He makes this clear at every turn, being completely rude and disrespectful to both Logan and Emily. He even goes as far as moving Emily’s ex, Tripp to New York to be Emily’s “roommate.”<br /><br />What follows is a lot of not much and then a ton of over the top drama toward the end. There were a lot of things that didn’t work for me in this book. First, I just found it kind of boring, there just was no meat to the story. It was a lot of sappy thoughts with the sex scenes thrown in and I kept waiting for something interesting to happen. And by interesting I DO NOT mean what ended up happening… <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I absolutely HATED the whole car accident thing and Logan being in a coma. It felt so contrived and after Logan got hit I actually stopped listening to my audiobook for a few hours. I was in my car, there was no reason I needed to stop. It just made me roll my eyes and I actually considered not even finishing after that. There is even a part when they are at a funeral (for the driver that hit Logan) and I know the intention is to shock and make you question whether it might be Logan’s funeral that Emily and his brothers are attending. This just annoyed me even more. I hate devices like this! I also thought the whole turn around with Emily’s dad was obnoxiously cheesy. I found it completely unrealistic and just way too much. I like Emily and I felt for everything she had gone through with her dad, so I do think she deserved an apology, but the way it was done felt so wrong. It didn’t feel special, it just felt really fake. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br /><br />When I realized toward the end of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18089551.Tall__Tatted_and_Tempting__The_Reed_Brothers___1_" title="Tall, Tatted and Tempting (The Reed Brothers, #1) by Tammy Falkner" rel="nofollow noopener">Tall, Tatted and Tempting</a> that Logan and Emily would be getting another book, I was kind of excited. After getting into this one though, it soon became clear to me that a second book for them was really unnecessary. TTT was a short book. I really wish there had just been a few more chapters added to it and maybe an epilogue to tie up their story. As much as I like both Logan and Emily I didn’t enjoy reading (listening to) this book. My favorite part was the interactions with the brothers and even though this was a bust for me, I am looking forward to checking out the books for the rest of the Reed Brothers. <br /><i>
  <blockquote>“I know you love her, and, hell, I love her too. And Matt would throw you off a bridge if he thought he could have her.” …<br />“Ew,” Matt complains. “I don’t like her like that.” He points a finger in my face. “But I will throw you off a bridge if you hurt her.”</blockquote>
</i><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="3569273932458486722" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer15211969611207823591">Smart, Sexy and Secretive by Tammy Falkner<br/>Series: The Reed Brothers<br/>Book #: 2<br/>Characters: Logan & Emily <br/>**Do not recommend reading without first reading the first half of Logan & Emily’s story in Tall, Tatted and Tempting<br/><br/><br/>Emily is returning to New York after sacrificing her wants for Logan’s brother Matt to get the care he needed, but this time she has an alley in her mother, even if her father is dead set against her settling for Logan.<br/><br/>Three months have passed since she fled, unsure if Logan was a</span>
  <span id="freeText15211969611207823591" style="display:none">Smart, Sexy and Secretive by Tammy Falkner<br />Series: The Reed Brothers<br />Book #: 2<br />Characters: Logan &amp; Emily <br />**Do not recommend reading without first reading the first half of Logan &amp; Emily’s story in Tall, Tatted and Tempting<br /><br /><br />Emily is returning to New York after sacrificing her wants for Logan’s brother Matt to get the care he needed, but this time she has an alley in her mother, even if her father is dead set against her settling for Logan.<br /><br />Three months have passed since she fled, unsure if Logan was able to hold on to faith that she’d return – three months of not being able to communicate with him due to him being deaf. But all of that fades away when she rushes to see him the minute she gets settled.<br /> <br />As Logan tries to claim Emily as his own, he has to combat her father and her ex that seems to keep getting in the way. Winning over her father seems to be an impossible feat, but lucky for Logan, Emily doesn’t need anyone’s approval when it comes to following her heart.<br /><br />In the second installment of this series and the completion of Logan’s story we get a book with all the feels! I loved watching these two come back together, loved seeing the love that these brothers share and even the softer moments between Emily and her parents... it all was just chopped full of feel good moments. <br /><br />It took me forever to get to this series but I just can’t stop myself from reading them now. Each brother has their own set of endearing qualities and back story that all blends so nicely together and although I loved Pete’s story and Logan was sitting pretty easily in the top spot... I think Matt’s heart is what I’m going to fall in love with the most. <br /><br />If you love a great series that is compiled of fantastic standalone novels, this is one to check out. It is filled to the brim with feels and is low on the angst and just gives you this happy feeling once you flip that last page. <br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer7585717092347237732">4 Standing Up For What You Believe Stars * * * *<br/><br/>This is the second installment in Tammy Falkner's Reed Brothers series. She has created a family of strong, real life men... we could meet any one of them some place if we were lucky. These men have heart, caring and sex appeal galore...but more importantly, the strength of them as a unit provides the ability for all of them to share their love with others. <br/><br/>We follow Emily and Logan in their young, fresh romance through their POVs. Genius. We exper</span>
  <span id="freeText7585717092347237732" style="display:none">4 Standing Up For What You Believe Stars * * * *<br><br>This is the second installment in Tammy Falkner's Reed Brothers series. She has created a family of strong, real life men... we could meet any one of them some place if we were lucky. These men have heart, caring and sex appeal galore...but more importantly, the strength of them as a unit provides the ability for all of them to share their love with others. <br><br>We follow Emily and Logan in their young, fresh romance through their POVs. Genius. We experience the hurdles her father throws at them by bringing in the pompous ass of the ex boyfriend. There are confrontations, manipulations and out and out insults aimed at Logan. He, though, knows what and who he wants; he is not intimidated by the family's money or status. <br><br>He has only one goal in mind... to make his life with Emily.<br><br>I am a huge fan now of this series. The humanity of it gets to me. Learning disabilities, hearing impairment... they are things to learn how to cope with and find alternatives and solutions. No pity parties or woe is me.... it is let's get on board and figure out how to live to the fullest. This is a positive attitude and should be with all things. It makes this such an asset to the storyline. <br><br>It also doesn't hurt that the couple is so great together. They fit... they are a unit and never run away from each other.<br><br>There is a continuing feel to these stories but not to the point of serious cliffys... it is more like the reader wanting to know what will happen now... with the other parts of the family. The layering of the secondary storyline with fleshed out characters enhance the overall reading, too.<br><br>There are more books in this series... revolving around one of the younger brothers, Pete. I will be jumping onto it next because I think I have adopted 5 brothers late in my life... <br><br><strong>For more reviews, Free E-books and Giveaways</strong><br><a href="http://starangelsreviews.blogspot.com" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

  <span id="freeText17246693868887920337" style="display:none">Emily and Logan's story continues in this follow-up to 'Tall, Tatted and Tempting'. This time around, they're up against Emily's conniving father and her douchebag ex-boyfriend. It seems that these two just can't take a hint and are determined to see Emily marry Tripp. A tragic accident changes everything and Emily's father is forced to reconsider the future he'd envisioned for Emily.<br /><br />Much like the first book, this second book was heart-warming and sweet. I listened to the audiobook version and the narration was good. I liked this follow-up and felt like it gave some closure after the abrupt change in events at the end of book 1. If you're interested in where Emily and Logan's relationship went after book 1, then you'll probably enjoy this one also.</span>

<tr class="no_border feedFooterReview" id="update_comment_stuff_Review1023014067">

<div id="review_715799238" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/715799238" />
    <a title="Vallsykes" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5164414-vallsykes"><img alt="Vallsykes" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1367067514p2/5164414.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/715799238?book_show_action=true">Sep 09, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Vallsykes" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Vallsykes" href="/user/show/5164414-vallsykes">Vallsykes</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">those who read Part 1</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5164414-vallsykes?shelf=multiple-or-dual-pov">multiple-or-dual-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5164414-vallsykes?shelf=beautifully-beta">beautifully-beta</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5164414-vallsykes?shelf=more-than-3-stars">more-than-3-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5164414-vallsykes?shelf=young-adult-erotica">young-adult-erotica</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5164414-vallsykes?shelf=new-adult-rave">new-adult-rave</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5164414-vallsykes?shelf=family-matters">family-matters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5164414-vallsykes?shelf=separation-plot">separation-plot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5164414-vallsykes?shelf=could-predict-the-ending">could-predict-the-ending</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5164414-vallsykes?shelf=hero-saved-the-story">hero-saved-the-story</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5164414-vallsykes?shelf=disability">disability</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer715799238" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13173874428706052198"><b>another 3.5 stars</b><br/><blockquote>
<i>"...my eighteen year old son asked me if he could read. But when we got to the “hot” parts, he asked me if I would cut them out. He asked me for a version “just for him.”</i><br/>Tammy Falkner</blockquote>Well, I'm not sure I know which version I read, but semi-dirty, smexi-talk was exhibited, a little, by the hero, Logan. (Again) still, I couldn't reconcile Neo-alpha-like Logan, the<i> I-get-down-with-the-low-down</i> Logan, with the Logan who is deaf and didn't talk for eight years. When his words come o</span>
  <span id="freeText13173874428706052198" style="display:none"><b>another 3.5 stars</b><br><blockquote>
<i>"...my eighteen year old son asked me if he could read. But when we got to the “hot” parts, he asked me if I would cut them out. He asked me for a version “just for him.”</i><br>Tammy Falkner</blockquote>Well, I'm not sure I know which version I read, but semi-dirty, smexi-talk was exhibited, a little, by the hero, Logan. (Again) still, I couldn't reconcile Neo-alpha-like Logan, the<i> I-get-down-with-the-low-down</i> Logan, with the Logan who is deaf and didn't talk for eight years. When his words come out...the most we get is that they're "soft" &amp; "quiet-like", so please <i>anyone</i>, feel my frustration when he is speaking his mind in longer than two sentences and I am absent descriptions of "raspy" "rough" "uneven pitches and tones" like he's trying his voice out or needs to repeat himself. That would have been more plausible.<br><br>The more Logan entrenches himself in Emily's life(<i>meeting her family</i>),the bolder he is portrayed. Only one time do we get someone reacting ignorantly towards Logan, a person shouting words at him like he is dumb, but this is not provoked by any embarrassing speech performance, just by the knowledge that his is deaf. I guess I would have liked a more realistic characterization of this aspect. Not that being deaf is a crux, but at times I forgot that he was deaf because he responded as if he weren't, in long speeches. Just one of my pet peeves when it comes to connecting with characters.<br><br>Anyway, in this sequel, Emily has faced her greatest fear and starts to try new things like enrolling in Julliard and learning sign.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380436109ra/881374.gif" width="240" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>It's relieves some of the implausibility when she and Jordan have moments of communication in sign. And even though I liked Emily a little more in this one, her character never outshines Logan's. It almost gets outdone by the side stories of Logan's brothers, Matt and Paul, threatening to steal a little of the main couple's thunder. The heart-tickling "family" love is ever present coupled with a bit of tease to get you interested in reading future stories.<br><br>In all, Logan and Emily stay together by the sweetness that is Emily and the sheer strength of determination that is Logan. The biggest conflict between them is Emily's rich autocratic father who makes some underhanded moves to undercut Logan. And Logan's reaction to this is at times impressive, but at the same time not as poignant as it was probably written to be. Emily and her father come to a turning point in their relationship, something of which happens belatedly and awkwardly. <br><br>Sooo, this sequel may not have been as lame as most I've read in the NA world, but it wasn't a sparkling surprise either. I'll just say that I didn't mind reading it one bit, at all.<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="13173874428706052198" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads?shelf=4-star-books">4-star-books</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer887323797" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15467573170552453602"><b>4.25 (YAY it’s still Emily and Logan’s Story) Stars</b><br/><br/>There will be spoilers from Book 1, Tall Tatted and Tempting.<br/><br/>Emily left Logan to save Matt. Who saw that coming right? She told the reporters that she will be back in NY. So its months later and Logan has waited and Emily is ready to be back with her man. <br/><br/>I LOVE that there is no separation! Yes, Smart, Sexy and Secretive was a bit short (not as short as book 1), but Tammy Falkner didn’t split them up! Usually this happens in book 2 in series.<br/><br/>Emi</span>
  <span id="freeText15467573170552453602" style="display:none"><b>4.25 (YAY it’s still Emily and Logan’s Story) Stars</b><br><br>There will be spoilers from Book 1, Tall Tatted and Tempting.<br><br>Emily left Logan to save Matt. Who saw that coming right? She told the reporters that she will be back in NY. So its months later and Logan has waited and Emily is ready to be back with her man. <br><br>I LOVE that there is no separation! Yes, Smart, Sexy and Secretive was a bit short (not as short as book 1), but Tammy Falkner didn’t split them up! Usually this happens in book 2 in series.<br><br>Emily is back to her old self, she’s blond, rich and going to school. Logan is still the poor guy living with his brothers. Emily’s father disapproves of Logan and Logan tries really hard to fit in Emily’s world.<br><br>I want to say how much I love there was JUST the right amount of angst, tension and light moments. I was never frustrated and didn’t want to pull my hair out. I love Logan’s and Emily’s love for each other. Yes, Emily is very different from Logan. Emily’s family can afford a private jet and it’s all about appearances. Logan doesn’t have the easiest life, but he lives it to his fullest and pursues what he loves.<br><br>Emily’s father has a huge presence in her life and even Trip comes back to add more conflict. I wish these books were longer, but just like book 1, I wasn’t disappointed. <br><br><b>Series Order</b><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18089551.Tall__Tatted_and_Tempting__The_Reed_Brothers___1_" title="Tall, Tatted and Tempting (The Reed Brothers, #1) by Tammy Falkner" rel="nofollow noopener">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1293177222" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3752184741407394797"><br/>Book 1 ended with Kat (real name Emily) leaving Logan and returning to SF.<br/>Now it's 3 months later, and Emily has gotten acceptance to go to Juliard and she secretly hopes that being in the same city (NYC) will reunite her with Logan. After all now he knows that she left him in accordance with the deal she made with her father to pay for the costly cancer treatments for Matt (Logan's older brother). Will he forgive her for just leaving him like that?<br/><br/>This one had a bit more sex than book 1, much t</span>
  <span id="freeText3752184741407394797" style="display:none"><br />Book 1 ended with Kat (real name Emily) leaving Logan and returning to SF.<br />Now it's 3 months later, and Emily has gotten acceptance to go to Juliard and she secretly hopes that being in the same city (NYC) will reunite her with Logan. After all now he knows that she left him in accordance with the deal she made with her father to pay for the costly cancer treatments for Matt (Logan's older brother). Will he forgive her for just leaving him like that?<br /><br />This one had a bit more sex than book 1, much to my dismay. I was concerned it would overshadow the story. I loved how committed Logan and Emily despite her father's best attempt to pair her with his protégé Tripp. <br /><br />The relationship between Logan and his 3 brothers remains the best thing in this book. Brothers have so much love and support, and they've embraced Emily. This isn't the typical tattoo artist/rocker romance I'm used to. I liked this story because character connection engaged me. The main characters were very likable and I was hopepeful for their future together. I like that peace was achieved and relationships were repaired. <br />The writing was enjoyable, and I plan to read more from this author in the future.<br /></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer890148413" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16597620518893760516">This is the continuation of Logan and Emily's story from Book 1 Tall, Tatted and Tempting. Emily came back to New York to enroll for Julliard and to reunite with Logan. There were some conflict with her dad and the appearance of her douche of an ex-boyfriend. <br/><br/>Honestly, I felt that Logan's story should have ended with a HEA at Book 1 because I can't wait to read about the rest of the Reed Brothers. In Book 2 I felt that Logan and Emily's story was drag on with more sexy times and some minor drama</span>
  <span id="freeText16597620518893760516" style="display:none">This is the continuation of Logan and Emily's story from Book 1 Tall, Tatted and Tempting. Emily came back to New York to enroll for Julliard and to reunite with Logan. There were some conflict with her dad and the appearance of her douche of an ex-boyfriend. <br /><br />Honestly, I felt that Logan's story should have ended with a HEA at Book 1 because I can't wait to read about the rest of the Reed Brothers. In Book 2 I felt that Logan and Emily's story was drag on with more sexy times and some minor drama thrown in. The silver lining to all that it is a pretty short and quick read, Logan and Emily's are a very strong couple, there isn't any silly misunderstanding or frustrating moment. You just can see how strong they are throughout the whole ordeal.<br /><br />This was quite an average read to catch up with Logan and Emily. I can only said that they were so perfect for each other. Now I just can't wait to get to Book 3 for Pete's story.<br /><br />P/s: There are two version in the ebook, Sexy and Sexy lite.</span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('CmE7HJXSYj2a3rbHXFEoTDJKGg6valrphOlxW7uUSyQW9LGn7Hvpc2VJZXx4uVfdC396CiOrEinojDTQViG2ow==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('RPwE/l0gHmNG3SPuaGvteJQ6mjPmphsAad4lHIwWxZxYaY5FJImVLblK8FVMg5LprQ/6N2pnU8AFu2CXYaM4Gw==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer6275464913570823889">Tammy Falkner lives on a farm in a lovely, sprawling little town in rural NC with her beekeeper husband and a house full of boys, a few dogs, and a cat or two (or five – who has time to count?). As half of the Lydia Dare team, she has co-written ten books, including the Westfield Wolves series and the Gentlemen Vampyre series. A huge fan of Regency England, she often wonders what other kinds of ma</span>
  <span id="freeText6275464913570823889" style="display:none">Tammy Falkner lives on a farm in a lovely, sprawling little town in rural NC with her beekeeper husband and a house full of boys, a few dogs, and a cat or two (or five – who has time to count?). As half of the Lydia Dare team, she has co-written ten books, including the Westfield Wolves series and the Gentlemen Vampyre series. A huge fan of Regency England, she often wonders what other kinds of magical, mythical and strange creatures might live and interact within the ton. Exploring the theory that the fae can walk between Regency England and their own land, Tammy spends as much time as possible with the lords and ladies of society, horse-drawn carriages, and elegant balls. Now add to that some faeries, a little murder, a bit of mayhem, and a troublesome garden gnome, and you have her exciting new series. She hopes you enjoys her world as much as she does.<br /><br />Also writes as<br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/3112090.Lydia_Dare" rel="nofollow noopener">Lydia Dare</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="6275464913570823889" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>
